881 ----
882 // DW_OP_LLVM_user has two operands: ----
883 // (1) An unsigned LEB128 "LLVM Vendor Extension Opcode". ----
884 // (2) Zero or more literal operands, the number and type of which are ----
885 // implied by the opcode (1). ----
886 // DW_OP_LLVM_user acts as an extension multiplexer, opening up the encoding ----
887 // space to accommodate an infinite number of extensions. This better reflects ----
888 // the de-facto permanent allocation of extensions. ----
889 HANDLE_DW_OP(0xe9, LLVM_user, 0, LLVM) 0
890 // "LLVM Vendor Extension" operations under the DW_OP_LLVM_user encoding ----
891 // scheme. This list is authoritative and exhaustive. Once an operation is ----
892 // registered here it cannot be removed nor have its encoding changed. The ----
893 // encoding space must skip zero (which is reserved) and have no gaps. ----
894 // ----
895 // The DW_OP_LLVM_user DW_OP_LLVM_nop operation has no effect on the ----
896 // location stack or any of its values. It is defined as a placeholder for ----
897 // testing purposes. ----
898 HANDLE_DW_OP_LLVM_USEROP(0x0001, nop) 0
